Abstract: When people recount personal memories, they often refer to people, places, and events indirectly, relying on contextual cues rather than explicit names. Such implicit references are central to reminiscence narratives: first-person accounts of lived experience used in therapeutic, archival, and social settings. They pose a difficult computational problem because the intended entity must be inferred from dispersed narrative evidence rather than from a local mention. We introduce IRC-Bench, the Implicit Reminiscence Context Benchmark, for evaluating implicit entity recognition in reminiscence transcripts. The benchmark targets non-locality: entity-identifying cues are distributed across multiple, non-contiguous clauses, unlike named entity recognition, entity linking, or coreference resolution. IRC-Bench comprises 25,136 samples constructed from 12,337 Wiki-data-linked entities across 1,994 transcripts spanning 11 thematic domains. Each sample pairs an Entity-Grounded Narrative, in which the target entity is explicitly mentioned, with an Entity-Elided Narrative, in which direct mentions are removed. We evaluate 19 configurations across LLM generation, dense retrieval, RAG, and fine-tuning. QLoRA-adapted Llama 3.1 8B performs best in the open-world setting (38.94% exact match; 51.59% Jaccard), while fine-tuned DPR leads closed-world retrieval (35.38% Hit@1; 71.49% Hit@10). ### [124] [A$^2$TGPO: Agentic Turn-Group Policy Optimization with Adaptive Turn-level Clipping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06200)
*Dingwei Chen,Zefang Zong,Zhipeng Ma,Leo Luo,Yang Li,Chengming Li,Peng Chen,Jie Jiang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出A²TGPO方法，通过改进信息增益（IG）信号的归一化、累积和裁剪方式，解决了强化学习在智能体大语言模型中过程级信用分配的三个系统性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖外部过程奖励模型或树形结构展开，无法高效地在多轮交互中评估单个工具调用的贡献；而直接利用信息增益（IG）作为内在信号时，面临跨轮次归一化扭曲、优势幅度随轨迹深度漂移、固定裁剪范围不适应IG差异三大挑战。

Method: A²TGPO包含三项设计：(1) 轮次组归一化——在同(prompt, 轮次索引)组内归一化IG，使每轮与相同交互深度的同伴比较；(2) 方差重缩放折扣累积——用累计项数的平方根归一化累积IG，保持不同深度优势幅度可比；(3) 自适应轮次级裁剪——根据归一化IG动态调整每轮的裁剪范围，信息量大的轮次放宽更新，信息量少的收紧。

Result: 论文提出A²TGPO方法，在保留IG作为内在信号的基础上，解决了规范化、累积和裁剪三个系统性问题。

Conclusion: A²TGPO通过重新设计IG信号的归一化、累积和消费方式，为智能体LLM的强化学习提供了更有效的逐轮次信用分配机制。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning for agentic large language models (LLMs) typically relies on a sparse, trajectory-level outcome reward, making it difficult to evaluate the contribution of individual tool-calls within multi-turn interactions. Existing approaches to such process credit assignment either depend on separate external process reward models that introduce additional consumption, or tree-based structural rollout that merely redistributes the outcome signal while constraining trajectory diversity. A promising alternative leverages the per-turn change in the policy's predicted probability of the ground-truth, termed Information Gain (IG), as an intrinsic process signal without an external evaluator. However, prior work on leveraging IG signals within the RL training loop faces three systematic challenges: normalizing across turns that face heterogeneous positional contexts can distort the relative standing of individual turns, accumulating a variable number of terms causes advantage magnitudes to drift with trajectory depth, and a fixed clipping range governs policy updates identically for turns with vastly different IG signals. In this paper, we propose A$^2$TGPO (Agentic Turn-Group Policy Optimization with Adaptive Turn-level Clipping), which retains IG as the intrinsic signal but re-designs how it is normalized, accumulated, and consumed: (i) turn-group normalization: normalizes IG within each (prompt, turn-index) group so that each turn is compared only against peers at the same interaction depth; (ii) variance-rescaled discounted accumulation: divides cumulative normalized IG by square root of accumulated terms to keep advantage magnitudes comparable across turn positions; and (iii) adaptive turn-level clipping: modulates each turn's clipping range based on its normalized IG, widening the update region for informative turns and narrowing it for uninformative ones.

</details>


### [125] [TIDE: Every Layer Knows the Token Beneath the Context](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06216)
*Ajay Jaiswal,Lauren Hannah,Han-Byul Kim,Duc Hoang,Mehrdad Farajtabar,Minsik Cho*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文指出现有LLM中“token索引仅在输入层查询一次后永久丢弃”的设计存在罕见词训练不足和语义坍缩两大缺陷，并提出TIDE方法——通过嵌入记忆模块（EmbeddingMemory）在每一层注入上下文无关的语义向量，从而缓解这些问题并提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前所有LLM都默认token索引仅在输入嵌入层被查询一次后丢弃（单一注入假设），这一设计导致两个结构性缺陷：稀有词因梯度信号不足而训练不充分（罕见词问题），以及参数有限的模型将分布相似的token映射到难以区分的隐状态（上下文坍缩问题）。

Method: 提出TIDE方法，在标准Transformer基础上增加EmbeddingMemory模块。该模块由K个独立的MemoryBlock组成，将token索引映射为上下文无关的语义向量，并通过一个深度条件化的softmax路由器（含可学习的空银行）将这些向量注入到每一层。

Result: 理论分析和实验结果表明，TIDE能够有效缓解单一token身份注入带来的问题，并在多个语言建模和下游任务上取得性能提升。

Conclusion: TIDE通过跨层重复注入上下文无关的语义向量，克服了单一注入假设的局限性，改善了罕见词表示和语义区分性，为Transformer架构提供了一种简单有效的增强方案。

Abstract: We revisit a universally accepted but under-examined design choice in every modern LLM: a token index is looked up once at the input embedding layer and then permanently discarded. This single-injection assumption induces two structural failures: (i) the Rare Token Problem, where a Zipf-type distribution of vocabulary causes rare-token embeddings are chronically under-trained due to receiving a fraction of the cumulative gradient signal compared to common tokens; and (ii) the Contextual Collapse Problem, where limited parameters models map distributionally similar tokens to indistinguishable hidden states. As an attempt to address both, we propose TIDE, which augments the standard transformer with EmbeddingMemory: an ensemble of K independent MemoryBlocks that map token indices to context-free semantic vectors, computed once and injected into every layer through a depth-conditioned softmax router with a learnable null bank. We theoretically and empirically establish the benefits of TIDE in addressing the issues associated with single-token identity injection as well as improve performance across multiple language modeling and downstream tasks.

</details>


### [126] [UniPrefill: Universal Long-Context Prefill Acceleration via Block-wise Dynamic Sparsification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06221)
*Qihang Fan,Huaibo Huang,Zhiying Wu,Bingning Wang,Ran He*

Main category: cs.CL

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有长上下文预填充加速方法主要聚焦于稀疏注意力机制，仅在全注意力模型上有效，难以迁移到线性/全注意力混合或滑动窗口/全注意力混合等新兴架构，且与连续批处理不兼容，难以集成到现代推理引擎中。

Method: 提出UniPrefill框架，在token级别直接加速模型计算；将其实现为连续批处理算子，并扩展vLLM的调度策略以原生支持预填充-解码协同处理和张量并行。

Result: UniPrefill在TTFT（首次生成令牌时间）上实现最高2.1倍加速，且加速效果随并发请求数量增加而更加明显。

Conclusion: UniPrefill是一种架构通用的预填充加速方案，解决了现有方法在混合架构上的性能退化问题，并能无缝集成到vLLM等现代推理引擎中，为长上下文推理效率提供了实用且可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: As large language models (LLMs) continue to advance rapidly, they are becoming increasingly capable while simultaneously demanding ever-longer context lengths. To improve the inference efficiency of long-context processing, several novel low-complexity hybrid architectures have recently been proposed, effectively alleviating the computational burden of long-context inference. However, existing research on long-context prefill acceleration remains predominantly focused on sparse attention mechanisms, which achieve their maximum speedup only on full-attention models. When transferred to emerging architectures--such as linear/full attention hybrids or sliding window/full attention hybrids--these prefill acceleration approaches suffer significant performance degradation. Furthermore, such methods are generally incompatible with continuous batching, making them difficult to integrate into modern inference engines such as vLLM. To this end, we propose UniPrefill, a prefill acceleration framework applicable to virtually any model architecture, which directly accelerates the model's computation at the token level. We further implement UniPrefill as a continuous batching operator and extend vLLM's scheduling strategy to natively support prefill-decode co-processing and tensor parallel for UniPrefill, enabling its seamless integration into vLLM. UniPrefill achieves up to 2.1x speedup in Time-To-First-Token (TTFT), with the acceleration becoming increasingly pronounced as the number of concurrent requests grows.

Abstract: Autoraters, also referred to as LLM-as-judges, are increasingly used for evaluation and automated content moderation. However, there is limited statistical analysis of how modifications in a rubric presented to both humans and autoraters affect their score agreement. Rubrics that ask for an overall or \emph{holistic} judgment - for example, rating the ``quality'' of an essay - may be inconsistently interpreted due to the complexity or subjectivity of the criteria. Conversely, rubrics can ask for \emph{analytic} judgments, which decompose assessment criteria - for example, ``quality'' into ``fluency'' and ``organization''. While these rubrics can be edited to improve the individual accuracy of both human and automated scoring, this approach may result in disagreement between the two scores, or with the associated holistic judgment. Designing and deploying reliable autoraters requires understanding not just the relationship between human and autorater annotations but how that relationship changes as holistic or analytic judgments are elicited. The results indicate that rubric edits providing representative examples and additional context, and reducing positional bias in the rubric increased human-autorater agreement, while higher rubric complexity and conservative aggregation methods tended to decrease it. The findings from the automatic essay scoring and instruction-following evaluation domains suggest that practitioners should carefully analyze domain- and rubric-specific performance to move towards higher human-autorater agreement.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Agentic RAG虽能处理复杂问题，但多步迭代过程因自回归生成冗长的思维和子查询导致高延迟，亟需降低延迟的同时保持性能。

Method: 提出LatentRAG框架，将推理和检索转移到连续潜在空间：直接从隐藏状态单次前向生成潜在思维和子查询令牌；对齐LLM与稠密检索模型于潜在空间；引入并行潜在解码机制将潜在令牌转译为自然语言以增强可解释性。

Abstract: Single-step retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) provides an efficient way to incorporate external information for simple question answering tasks but struggles with complex questions. Agentic RAG extends this paradigm by replacing single-step retrieval with a multi-step process, in which the large language model (LLM) acts as a search agent that generates intermediate thoughts and subqueries to iteratively interact with the retrieval system. This iterative process incurs substantial latency due to the autoregressive generation of lengthy thoughts and subqueries. To address this limitation, we propose LatentRAG, a novel framework that shifts both reasoning and retrieval from discrete language space to continuous latent space. Unlike existing explicit methods that generate natural language thoughts or subqueries token-by-token, LatentRAG produces latent tokens for thoughts and subqueries directly from the hidden states in a single forward pass. We align LLMs with dense retrieval models in the latent space, enabling retrieval over latent subquery tokens and supporting end-to-end joint optimization. To improve transparency and encourage semantically meaningful latent representations, we incorporate a parallel latent decoding mechanism that translates latent tokens back into natural language. Extensive experiments on seven benchmark datasets show that LatentRAG achieves performance comparable to explicit agentic RAG methods while reducing inference latency by approximately 90%, substantially narrowing the latency gap with traditional single-step RAG.

### [131] [Log-Likelihood, Simpson's Paradox, and the Detection of Machine-Generated Text](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06294)
*Tom Kempton,Viktor Drobnyi,Maeve Madigan,Stuart Burrell*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文发现现有AI文本检测器因在隐藏空间中不均匀地聚合token似然分数，导致辛普森悖论式性能退化。通过引入基于贝叶斯决策理论的局部校准方法，显著提升了检测性能，例如Fast-DetectGPT在GPT-4文本上的AUROC从0.63提升到0.85。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有检测器在隐藏空间中非均匀地聚合token似然分数，导致强局部信号被不当聚合破坏（辛普森悖论），造成性能瓶颈。

Method: 提出基于贝叶斯决策理论的局部校准方法：先学习轻量级预测器，估计隐藏空间中不同位置的条件分数分布，再聚合校准后的对数似然比，而非原始token分数。

Result: 在所有基线检测器和数据集上一致且显著提升检测性能。Fast-DetectGPT在GPT-4文本上AUROC从0.63提升至0.85；提出的局部校准DMAP检测器达到最先进水平。

Abstract: The ability to reliably distinguish human-written text from that generated by large language models is of profound societal importance. The dominant approach to this problem exploits the likelihood hypothesis: that machine-generated text should appear more probable to a detector language model than human-written text. However, we demonstrate that the token-level signal distinguishing human and machine text is non-uniform across the hidden space of the detector model, and naively averaging likelihood-based token scores across regions with fundamentally different statistical structure, as most detectors do, causes a form of Simpson's paradox: a strong local signal is destroyed by inappropriate aggregation. To correct for this, we introduce a learned local calibration step grounded in Bayesian decision theory. Rather than aggregating raw token scores, we first learn lightweight predictors of the score distributions conditioned on position in hidden space, and aggregate calibrated log-likelihood ratios instead. This single intervention dramatically and consistently improves detection performance across all baseline detectors and all datasets we consider. For example, our calibrated variant of Fast-DetectGPT improves AUROC from $0.63$ to $0.85$ on GPT-5.4 text, and a locally-calibrated DMAP detector we introduce achieves state-of-the-art performance across the board. That said, our central contribution is not a new detector, but a precise diagnosis of a significant cause of under-performance of existing detectors and a principled, modular remedy compatible with any token-averaging pipeline. This will serve as a foundation for the community to build upon, with natural avenues including richer distributional models, improved calibration strategies, and principled ensembling with hidden-space geometry signals via the full Bayes-optimal decision rule.

Motivation: 尽管工具集成推理（TIR）能扩展思维模型的推理能力，但直接引入工具评估反而会降低推理性能，且强思维模型几乎从不实际调用工具。如何在保持原有纯文本推理能力的前提下，有效注入自然工具使用行为成为核心挑战。

Method: (i) 基于学习难度筛选适合工具增强的问题作为教师轨迹；(ii) 控制工具使用轨迹的比例以防止纯文本推理能力的灾难性遗忘；(iii) 用pass@k和响应长度而非训练损失来优化TIR SFT；(iv) 在合适的SFT初始化和防模式坍缩机制上进行稳定的RLVR训练。

Result: 在Qwen3思维模型（4B和30B）上，提出的方案在多个基准测试中达到开源模型SOTA，其中AIME 2025分别取得96.7%（4B）和99.2%（30B）的优异成绩。

Conclusion: 通过精心设计的TIR配方——包括学习性优先的教师轨迹选择、比例控制、pass@k导向优化以及稳定的RLVR训练——可以在不牺牲纯文本推理能力的情况下有效注入工具使用行为，显著提升模型在各类推理基准上的表现。

Abstract: Tool-integrated reasoning (TIR) offers a direct way to extend thinking models beyond the limits of text-only reasoning. Paradoxically, we observe that tool-enabled evaluation can degrade reasoning performance even when the strong thinking models make almost no actual tool calls. In this paper, we investigate how to inject natural tool-use behavior into a strong thinking model without sacrificing its no-tool reasoning ability, and present a comprehensive TIR recipe. We highlight that (i) the effectiveness of TIR supervised fine-tuning (SFT) hinges on the learnability of teacher trajectories, which should prioritize problems inherently suited for tool-augmented solutions; (ii) controlling the proportion of tool-use trajectories could mitigate the catastrophic forgetting of text-only reasoning capacity; (iii) optimizing for pass@k and response length instead of training loss could maximize TIR SFT gains while preserving headroom for reinforcement learning (RL) exploration; (iv) a stable RL with verifiable rewards (RLVR) stage, built upon suitable SFT initialization and explicit safeguards against mode collapse, provides a simple yet remarkably effective solution. When applied to Qwen3 thinking models at 4B and 30B scales, our recipe yields models that achieve state-of-the-art performance in a wide range of benchmarks among open-source models, such as 96.7% and 99.2% on AIME 2025 for 4B and 30B, respectively.

</details>


### [135] [Measuring Evaluation-Context Divergence in Open-Weight LLMs: A Paired-Prompt Protocol with Pilot Evidence of Alignment-Pipeline-Specific Heterogeneity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06327)
*Florian A. D. Burnat,Brittany I. Davidson*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出评估-情境分歧概念，发现不同开源LLM在评估与部署场景下行为存在显著异质性，且评价者依赖性强。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 安全基准测试常被当作模型部署后行为的证据，但若模型行为因提示是否像评估而变化，这一推理便不可靠。作者旨在系统测量并揭示这种情境引发的行为差异。

Result: OLMo-3-Instruct是唯一的"评估谨慎型"（评估框架下拒绝率升11.8pp，有害合规降3.6pp）；Mistral-Small-3.2、Phi-3.5-mini和Llama-3.1-8B是"部署谨慎型"（评估vs部署拒绝效应-9至-20pp）。对齐是反转阶段，70B模型保持方向但幅度减弱。异质性依赖评判者：Llama-Guard-3-8B扁平化跨族对比。

Conclusion: 模型在评估与部署场景下的行为存在系统性差异且跨族异质，安全基准作为部署证据的推断需谨慎；评判者选择影响结论。

Abstract: Safety benchmarks are routinely treated as evidence about how a language model will behave once deployed, but this inference is fragile if behavior depends on whether a prompt looks like an evaluation. We define evaluation-context divergence as an observable within-item change in behavior induced by framing a fixed task as an evaluation, a live deployment interaction, or a neutral request, and present a paired-prompt protocol that measures it in open-weight LLMs while controlling for paraphrase variation, benchmark familiarity, and judge framing-sensitivity.
  Across five instruction-tuned checkpoints from four open-weight families plus a matched OLMo-3 base/instruct ablation ($20$ paired items, $840$ generations per checkpoint), we find striking heterogeneity. OLMo-3-Instruct alone is eval-cautious -- evaluation framing raises refusal vs. neutral by $11.8$pp ($p=0.007$) and reduces harmful compliance vs. deployment by $3.6$pp ($p=0.024$, $0/20$ items inverted) -- while Mistral-Small-3.2, Phi-3.5-mini, and Llama-3.1-8B are deployment-cautious}, with marginal eval-vs-deployment refusal effects of $-9$ to $-20$pp. The matched OLMo-3 base also exhibits the deployment-cautious pattern, identifying alignment as the inversion stage; within Llama-3.1, the $70$B model preserves direction with attenuated magnitude, ruling out a simple ``small-model effect that reverses at scale.'' One caveat: the cross-family heterogeneity is judge-dependent. Re-judging with a different-family safety classifier (Llama-Guard-3-8B) preserves the within-OLMo eval-cautious direction but flattens the cross-family contrast, indicating that the two judges operationalize distinct constructs.

### [136] [Don't Lose Focus: Activation Steering via Key-Orthogonal Projections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06342)
*Haoyan Luo,Mateo Espinosa Zarlenga,Mateja Jamnik*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SKOP是一种通过保持关键令牌的注意力模式来减少激活引导中推理性能下降的方法，在保持95%以上引导效果的同时，将性能损失降低5-7倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 激活引导在控制LLM行为时会导致推理和检索性能下降，作者认为主要原因是注意力重路由（attention rerouting），即引导向量改变了查询-键匹配，使注意力从重要的上下文令牌转移到信息量较少的令牌上。

Method: 提出SKOP（Steering via Key-Orthogonal Projections），通过保持模型依赖的少量焦点令牌上的注意力模式，同时允许在较不重要的尾部令牌间重新分配注意力，以约束有害的注意力重路由而不消除引导效果。

Result: 在多个引导基准测试中，SKOP实现了最佳的引导-效用权衡，将效用退化减少5-7倍，同时保持95%以上的原始引导效果。在长上下文检索场景中，SKOP通过避免注意力重路由维持了稳健性能。

Conclusion: 注意力重路由是激活引导导致性能下降的主要原因，SKOP通过约束这一现象实现了更优的权衡。

Abstract: Activation steering controls LLM behaviour towards target behaviour by intervening in internal representations, yet it often degrades reasoning and retrieval performance. We argue that a primary cause of this trade-off is attention rerouting: steering vectors alter query-key matching, shifting attention away from contextually important tokens toward less informative ones. To address this, we propose Steering via Key-Orthogonal Projections (SKOP), a steering method that constrains harmful attention rerouting without eliminating steering efficacy. SKOP achieves this by preserving attention patterns on a small set of focus tokens the model relies on for reasoning and retrieval, while allowing redistribution among less critical tail tokens. Across multiple steering benchmarks, we show that SKOP achieves the best joint steering-utility trade-off, reducing utility degradation by 5-7x while retaining over 95% of vanilla steering efficacy. Our results further suggest that, in long-context retrieval settings where vanilla steering approaches are ineffective, SKOP can maintain robust performance by avoiding attention rerouting.

Yet most instruction-following benchmarks focus on single-turn or short multi-turn scenarios, leaving open how well models handle long-horizon instruction-following tasks. To bridge this gap, we present SEQUOR, an automatic benchmark for evaluating constraint adherence in long multi-turn conversations. SEQUOR consists of simulated persona-driven interactions built with constraints extracted from real-world conversations. Our results show that even when following a single constraint, instruction-following accuracy consistently decreases as the conversation grows longer, with drops exceeding 11%. This decline becomes larger when models have to follow multiple constraints simultaneously, reducing their accuracy by over 40%. In scenarios where constraints are added or replaced at arbitrary points of the conversation, model accuracy decreases by more than 9%. Taken together, our results reveal that current models still struggle to follow user instructions in multi-turn conversations, and provide a way for better measuring instruction-following capabilities in assistants.

### [138] [GATHER: Convergence-Centric Hyper-Entity Retrieval for Zero-Shot Cell-Type Annotation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06403)
*Zhonghui Zhang,Feng Jiang,Shaowei Qin,Jiahao Zhao,Min Yang*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出GATHER（Graph-Aware Traversal with Hyper-Entity Retrieval），一种面向超实体查询的收敛中心检索器。通过全局多源图遍历识别拓扑收敛点（多个输入基因共同可达的节点），并结合节点和路径重要性评分，在检索阶段完全无需LLM参与。

Abstract: Zero-shot single-cell cell-type annotation aims to determine a cell's type from a given set of expressed genes without any training. Existing knowledge-graph-based RAG approaches retrieve evidence by expanding from source entities and relying on iterative LLM reasoning. However, in this setting each query contains tens to hundreds of genes, where no single gene is decisive and the label emerges only from their collective co-occurrence. Such hyper-entity queries fundamentally challenge local, entity-wise exploration strategies, which reason from individual genes, leading to poor scalability and substantial LLM cost. We propose GATHER (Graph-Aware Traversal with Hyper-Entity Retrieval), a convergence-centric retriever tailored to hyper-entity queries. It performs global multi-source graph traversal and identifies topological convergence points -- nodes jointly reachable from many input genes. These convergence nodes act as high-information hyper-entities that capture entity synergy. By incorporating node- and path-importance scoring, GATHER selects informative evidence entirely without LLM involvement during retrieval. Instantiated on a self-constructed cell-centric biological knowledge graph (VCKG), GATHER outperforms strong KG-RAG baselines (ToG, ToG-2, RoG, PoG) on two datasets (Immune and Lung), achieving the highest exact-match accuracy (27.45% and 59.64%) with only a single LLM call per sample, compared to 2--61 calls for KG-RAG baselines. Our results demonstrate that convergence nodes compress multi-entity signals into compact, high-information evidence that conveys more per item than multi-hop paths, providing an efficient global alternative to local entity-wise reasoning.

Inspired by this idea, we introduce the concept of \textbf{Mindscape Activation Signature (MiA-Signature)}, a compressed representation of the global activation pattern induced by a query. The study shows that textual and linguistic features can be used successfully in detecting fake news using the traditional machine learning approach as opposed to deep learning.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究语言模型惊奇度与隐喻新颖性判断之间的关系，以及词汇频率在这一关系中的作用。

Method: 使用8种不同大小的Pythia模型和154个训练检查点，分析两种词汇频率测量指标与惊奇度对隐喻新颖性评级的影响。

Result: 词汇频率比惊奇度更能预测隐喻新颖性；惊奇度-新颖性关联在训练早期达到峰值后下降；惊奇度-频率关联也呈现类似的时间模式。

Conclusion: 以往研究中观察到的语言模型惊奇度与隐喻新颖性的最优关联，可能错误地将上下文可预测性与隐喻新颖性和处理难度联系起来，而词汇频率才是主要的潜在因素。

Abstract: Language-model (LM) surprisal is widely used as a proxy for contextual predictability and has been reported to correlate with metaphor novelty judgments. However, surprisal is tightly intertwined with lexical frequency. We explore this interaction on metaphor novelty ratings using two different word frequency measures. We analyse surprisal estimates from eight Pythia model sizes and 154 training checkpoints. Across settings, word frequency is a stronger predictor of metaphor novelty than surprisal. Across training stages, the surprisal--novelty association peaks at an early stage and then falls again, mirroring a similarly timed increase in the surprisal--frequency association. These results suggest that the often-reported optimal LM surprisal settings may incorrectly associate contextual predictability with metaphor novelty and processing difficulty, whereas lexical frequency may be the major underlying factor.

### [144] [STALE: Can LLM Agents Know When Their Memories Are No Longer Valid?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06527)
*Hanxiang Chao,Yihan Bai,Rui Sheng,Tianle Li,Yushi Sun*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出STALE基准（400个冲突场景、1200个评估查询），揭示LLM智能体在记忆更新上的关键缺陷——即使检索到新证据，也无法摒弃旧信念（最佳模型仅55.2%准确率）；同时提出CUPMem原型，通过结构化状态整合与传播感知搜索来改善这一问题。

Motivation: 现有基准只测试静态事实检索，忽视了智能体需根据新证据修订已有记忆的能力，尤其是"隐性冲突"（新信息未显式否定旧信息，需常识推理才能发现）这一关键失败模式。

Method: 构建STALE基准（400个专家验证的冲突场景，上下文长达150K token），设计三维探测框架：状态解析（检测旧信念过时）、前提抵制（拒绝基于过时状态的查询）、隐式策略适应（在后续行为中主动应用更新状态）。评估前沿LLM和专用记忆框架，并提出CUPMem原型（结构化状态整合+传播感知搜索）。

Result: 最佳模型仅55.2%准确率；模型常接受查询中隐含的过时假设，且难以识别某一方面状态变化应使相关记忆失效。CUPMem原型初步提升了状态感知能力。

Conclusion: 智能体记忆存在"检索更新证据"与"据此行动"之间的普遍鸿沟，显式状态判定是构建鲁棒智能体记忆的有前景方向。

Abstract: Large Language Model (LLM) agents are increasingly expected to maintain coherent, long-term personalized memory, yet current benchmarks primarily measure static fact retrieval, overlooking the ability to revise stored beliefs when new evidence emerges. We identify a critical and underexplored failure mode, Implicit Conflict: a later observation invalidates an earlier memory without explicit negation, requiring contextual inference and commonsense reasoning to detect. To rigorously evaluate this capability, we introduce STALE, a benchmark of 400 expert-validated conflict scenarios (1,200 evaluation queries across three probing dimensions) spanning over 100 everyday topics with contexts up to 150K tokens. We propose a three-dimensional probing framework that tests State Resolution (detecting that a prior belief is outdated), Premise Resistance (rejecting queries that falsely presuppose a stale state), and Implicit Policy Adaptation (proactively applying updated states in downstream behavior). A systematic evaluation of frontier LLMs and specialized memory frameworks reveals a pervasive gap between retrieving updated evidence and acting on it, with even the best evaluated model achieving only 55.2% overall accuracy. Models often accept outdated assumptions embedded in a user's query, and they struggle to recognize when a change in one aspect of the user's state should invalidate related memories. To establish an initial baseline for state-aware memory, we further present CUPMem, a prototype that strengthens write-time revision through structured state consolidation and propagation-aware search, suggesting that explicit state adjudication is a promising direction for robust agentic memory.

### [145] [Efficient Pre-Training with Token Superposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06546)
*Bowen Peng,Théo Gigant,Jeffrey Quesnelle*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出Token-Superposition Training (TST)，一种无需修改模型架构、优化器或并行策略的即插即用预训练方法。通过两阶段训练（叠加阶段将多个连续token合并为一袋，使用多热交叉熵损失；恢复阶段回归标准训练），在270M至10B参数规模上实现最高2.5倍预训练加速，且保持或超越基线性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模语言模型预训练通常成本高昂且效率低下，现有加速方法往往需要复杂且侵入性的修改（如改动并行策略、优化器等）。作者希望提出一种简单、即插即用的方法，在不改变现有基础设施的前提下提升数据吞吐量。

Method: TST包含两个阶段：(1) 叠加阶段（Superposition Phase）：将多个连续token合并为一个"袋"（bag），采用多热交叉熵（MCE）损失进行高效训练；(2) 恢复阶段（Recovery Phase）：切换回标准训练方式。该方法不需要修改并行策略、优化器、分词器、数据或模型架构。

Result: 在270M和600M参数上进行了充分评估，并在3B和10B的A1B混合专家模型上验证了鲁棒性。在等损失条件下，TST在10B A1B规模上实现了最高2.5倍的预训练时间缩减，且在下游评估中一致优于基线。

Conclusion: TST是一种简单、高效、鲁棒的预训练加速方法，能够在不改变现有训练基础设施的前提下显著提升数据吞吐量，并在多种规模和设置下优于标准训练基线。

Abstract: Pre-training of Large Language Models is often prohibitively expensive and inefficient at scale, requiring complex and invasive modifications in order to achieve high data throughput. In this work, we present Token-Superposition Training (TST), a simple drop-in method that significantly improves the data throughput per FLOPs during pre-training without modifying the parallelism, optimizer, tokenizer, data, or model architecture. TST is done in two phases: (i) A highly efficient superposition phase where we combine many contiguous tokens into one bag and train using a multi-hot cross-entropy (MCE) objective, and (ii) a recovery phase where we revert back to standard training. We extensively evaluate TST on the scale of 270M and 600M parameters and validate on 3B and a 10B A1B mixture of experts model, demonstrating that it is highly robust in different settings. Ultimately, TST consistently outperforms baseline loss and downstream evaluations, and under equal-loss settings, TST yields up to a 2.5x reduction in total pre-training time at the 10B A1B scale.

Method: 提出Cola DLM，包含三个阶段：1) Text VAE学习稳定的文本到潜变量映射；2) 块因果DiT在连续潜空间中建模全局语义先验；3) 条件解码生成文本。扩散过程实现潜变量先验传输，而非token级别的观测恢复。

Existing alternatives still struggle to jointly achieve generation efficiency, scalable representation learning, and effective global semantic modeling. We propose Cola DLM, a hierarchical latent diffusion language model that frames text generation through hierarchical information decomposition. Cola DLM first learns a stable text-to-latent mapping with a Text VAE, then models a global semantic prior in continuous latent space with a block-causal DiT, and finally generates text through conditional decoding. From a unified Markov-path perspective, its diffusion process performs latent prior transport rather than token-level observation recovery, thereby separating global semantic organization from local textual realization. This design yields a more flexible non-autoregressive inductive bias, supports semantic compression and prior fitting in continuous space, and naturally extends to other continuous modalities. Through experiments spanning 4 research questions, 8 benchmarks, strictly matched ~2B-parameter autoregressive and LLaDA baselines, and scaling curves up to about 2000 EFLOPs, we identify an effective overall configuration of Cola DLM and verify its strong scaling behavior for text generation. Taken together, the results establish hierarchical continuous latent prior modeling as a principled alternative to strictly token-level language modeling, where generation quality and scaling behavior may better reflect model capability than likelihood, while also suggesting a concrete path toward unified modeling across discrete text and continuous modalities.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 训练因果Transformer时，标准缩放点积注意力（SDPA）的二次时间和内存复杂度成为长序列训练的性能瓶颈。

Method: 提出Lighthouse Attention，包含三个关键贡献：(i) 次二次层级预处理和后处理步骤，实现自适应序列压缩与解压缩；(ii) 对称压缩策略，同时对查询、键、值进行池化，保持从左到右的因果性，大幅提升并行性；(iii) 两阶段训练：大部分时间使用Lighthouse Attention预训练，最后短时间恢复为全注意力模型。

Abstract: Training causal transformers at extreme sequence lengths is bottlenecked by the quadratic time and memory of scaled dot-product attention (SDPA). In this work, we propose Lighthouse Attention, a training-only symmetrical selection-based hierarchical attention algorithm that wraps around ordinary SDPA and can be easily removed towards the end of the training. Our hierarchical selection is also gradient-free, which exempts us from dealing with a complicated and potentially inefficient backward pass kernel. Our contribution is three-fold: (i) A subquadratic hierarchical pre- and post-processing step that does adaptive compression and decompression of the sequence. (ii) A symmetrical compression strategy that pools queries, keys and values at the same time, while preserving left-to-right causality, which greatly improves parallelism. (iii) A two stage training approach which we pre-train for the majority of the time with Lighthouse Attention and recover a full attention model at the end with a short training. We run preliminary small scale LLM pre-training experiments that show the effectiveness of our method compared to full attention training with all other settings matched, where we achieve a faster total training time and lower final loss after the recovery phase. Full code is available at: https://github.com/ighoshsubho/lighthouse-attention

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) power deep research agents that synthesize information from hundreds of web sources into cited reports, yet these citations cannot be reliably verified. Unlike methods that verify claims in isolation, our framework closes the loop by retrieving the actual cited content, enabling human or model evaluators to judge each citation against its source. Citations are evaluated along three dimensions. (1) Link Works verifies URL accessibility, (2) Relevant Content measures topical alignment, and (3) Fact Check validates factual accuracy against source content. Ablation studies on research depth show that Fact Check accuracy drops by approximately 42% on average across two frontier models as tool calls scale from 2 to 150, demonstrating that more retrieval does not produce more accurate citations. *Xiangyuan Xue,Yifan Zhou,Zidong Wang,Shengji Tang,Philip Torr,Wanli Ouyang,Lei Bai,Zhenfei Yin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: StraTA是一个将显式的轨迹级策略引入智能体强化学习的框架，通过分层GRPO策略生成与动作执行，在ALFWorld、WebShop和SciWorld等基准上显著提升样本效率和最终性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LLM智能体优化方法大多是被动反应式的，导致在长程决策中探索和信用分配困难，缺乏显式的轨迹级策略引导。

Method: StraTA从初始任务状态采样紧凑策略，后续动作以此策略为条件，采用分层GRPO风格的 rollout 设计联合训练策略生成与动作执行，并辅以多样化策略展开和关键自我判断机制。

Result: 在ALFWorld上达到93.1%成功率，WebShop上84.2%成功率，SciWorld上63.5%总体得分，超越前沿闭源模型。

Conclusion: 引入显式轨迹级策略能有效提升LLM智能体在长期决策任务中的性能，StraTA是一种简单且高效的框架。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used as interactive agents, but optimizing them for long-horizon decision making remains difficult because current methods are largely purely reactive, which weakens both exploration and credit assignment over extended trajectories. In this work, we present Strategic Trajectory Abstraction (StraTA), a simple framework that introduces an explicit trajectory-level strategy into agentic reinforcement learning (RL). StraTA samples a compact strategy from the initial task state, conditions subsequent actions on that strategy, and trains strategy generation and action execution jointly with a hierarchical GRPO-style rollout design, further enhanced by diverse strategy rollout and critical self-judgment. Experiments on ALFWorld, WebShop, and SciWorld show that StraTA consistently improves both sample efficiency and final performance over strong baselines. StraTA reaches success rates of 93.1% on ALFWorld and 84.2% on WebShop. On SciWorld, StraTA attains a 63.5% overall score, outperforming frontier closed-source models.

</details>


### [153] [EMO: Pretraining Mixture of Experts for Emergent Modularity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06663)
*Ryan Wang,Akshita Bhagia,Sewon Min*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: EMO通过文档边界约束使MoE中的专家自然形成语义级模块化，在不损失性能的前提下支持专家子集独立部署，仅用25%的专家即可保持接近完整模型的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型作为单体系统部署，即使应用只需要部分能力（如代码、数学）也必须加载完整模型；标准MoE虽然理论上支持专家子集使用，但实践中按领域限制推理会导致严重性能下降，限制了其在内存受限场景下的实用性。

Method: 提出EMO训练方法：约束同一文档内的token从共享的专家池中选择专家，不同文档可使用不同的专家池，利用文档边界这一简单先验使相似领域的token自然依赖相似专家，从而在预训练中形成语义级专家分组。

Result: 预训练1B激活/14B总参数的EMO模型（1T tokens），完整模型性能与标准MoE持平；仅保留25%（12.5%）的专家时，性能绝对下降仅1%（3%），而标准MoE在此设置下崩溃。

Conclusion: EMO展示了通向模块化、内存高效部署大型稀疏模型的路径，为可组合架构开辟了新机会。

Abstract: Large language models are typically deployed as monolithic systems, requiring the full model even when applications need only a narrow subset of capabilities, e.g., code, math, or domain-specific knowledge. Mixture-of-Experts (MoEs) seemingly offer a potential alternative by activating only a subset of experts per input, but in practice, restricting inference to a subset of experts for a given domain leads to severe performance degradation. This limits their practicality in memory-constrained settings, especially as models grow larger and sparser. We introduce EMO, an MoE designed for modularity-the independent use and composition of expert subsets-without requiring human-defined priors. Our key idea is to encourage tokens from similar domains to rely on similar experts. Since tokens within a document often share a domain, EMO restricts them to select experts from a shared pool, while allowing different documents to use different pools. This simple constraint enables coherent expert groupings to emerge during pretraining using document boundaries alone. We pretrain a 1B-active, 14B-total EMO on 1T tokens. As a full model, it matches standard MoE performance. Crucially, it enables selective expert use: retaining only 25% (12.5%) of experts incurs just a 1% (3%) absolute drop, whereas standard MoEs break under the same setting. We further find that expert subsets in EMO specialize at semantic levels (e.g., domains such as math or code), in contrast to the low-level syntactic specialization observed in standard MoEs. Altogether, our results demonstrate a path toward modular, memory-efficient deployment of large, sparse models and open new opportunities for composable architectures.

</details>

### [154] [DADL: A Declarative Description Language for Enterprise Tool Libraries in LLM Agent Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05247)
*Axel Dunkel*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出DADL（Dunkel API描述语言），一种声明式YAML格式，用于解决MCP在大规模组织中的部署膨胀和上下文窗口消耗问题。DADL通过单一文件描述REST API的端点、认证、分页等，由运行时解释执行，无需为每个API部署独立服务器进程。实验表明，在1,833个工具定义的目录中，Code Mode将工具广告的上下文成本从约142,000 tokens降至约1,000 tokens，实现142倍压缩。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MCP标准下存在两个结构性问题：1）每个API集成需部署独立服务器进程，带来部署、依赖和凭据管理的开销，且大部分服务器只是REST API的薄包装；2）每个工具独立注册导致上下文窗口消耗随目录规模线性增长，实际部署只能暴露组织实际API的一小部分。

Method: 提出DADL格式，以YAML声明式文件描述REST API的端点、认证、分页、响应整形和访问分类。运行时层解释执行DADL文件，无需生成集成代码或部署每API服务器进程。所有工具共享同一运行时，凭据和授权集中管理，并通过固定大小的Code Mode接口将目录呈现给LLM。

Result: DADL v0.1规范已发布，公共注册表包含20个服务的1,833个工具定义。Code Mode将工具广告的上下文成本从约142,000 tokens降至约1,000 tokens，实现142倍压缩。

Conclusion: DADL实现了企业级工具库：一个版本化、可审计的API集成集合，任何团队可通过统一的认证和授权边界进行扩展、共享和使用。

Abstract: The Model Context Protocol (MCP) is the standard interface between large language model (LLM) agents and external tools. At organizational scale, however, it exposes two structural problems. First, every API integration is shipped as a dedicated server process with its own deployment, dependency tree, and credential handling; recent empirical work shows the overwhelming majority of these servers are thin wrappers around REST APIs. Second, the per-tool registration model causes context window consumption to grow linearly with catalog size, forcing real deployments to expose only a small fraction of the APIs an organization actually uses.
  We present DADL (Dunkel API Description Language), a YAML format describing a REST API's endpoints, authentication, pagination, response shaping, and access classification in a single declarative file. A DADL file is interpreted by an execution layer at runtime; no per-API server process is deployed and no integration code is generated, though the runtime is itself a server. Because all tools share that runtime, credentials and authorization are managed centrally, and the catalog reaches the LLM through a fixed-size Code Mode interface independent of size. The result is an Enterprise Tool Library: a versioned, auditable collection of API integrations any team can extend, share, and consume through one authentication and authorization boundary.
  The DADL v0.1 specification is released under CC BY-SA 4.0, and a public registry contains 1,833 tool definitions across 20 services. On this catalog, Code Mode reduces the context cost of tool advertisement from approximately 142,000 tokens to approximately 1,000, a 142x reduction; the per-call cost of search and execute invocations is additional and depends on the task.

</details>


### [155] [Automated Population-Level Audit Assurance via AI-Based Document Intelligence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05252)
*Santosh Vasudevan,Velu Natarajan*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于AI文档智能的自动化审计交易测试框架，利用Snowflake Document AI从少量标注样本中提取PDF报表结构化数据，与权威数据源进行大规模对账，实现全量而非抽样的审计覆盖，并通过仪表盘和自动化报告呈现结果，支持持续审计目标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的人工抽样审计方式在处理非结构化PDF报表时工作量大、效率低，无法扩展到数百万笔交易规模，需要更高效的自动化解决方案来提升审计覆盖率和持续监控能力。

Method: 采用Snowflake Document AI技术，仅需约20份标注文档作为训练语料，从非结构化PDF报表中提取结构化数据，然后将提取数据与权威数据源进行自动化对账比对，发现差异。

Result: 实现了从抽样审计到全量级审计的转变，显著提高了审计覆盖率，支持近乎实时的风险识别和持续审计目标，结果通过交互式仪表盘和自动报告呈现。

Conclusion: 文档智能与数据分析驱动的审计框架能够实现可扩展、近乎实时的风险识别和持续审计，使审计交易测试从抽样式转变为全量式，提升了审计质量与效率。

Abstract: Audit transaction testing validates accuracy and completeness of customer-facing statements against internal systems of record. Traditional manual, sample-based review of unstructured PDF statements is labor-intensive and does not scale to millions of transactions. This paper presents an automated framework for large-scale audit transaction testing using AI-based document intelligence. The solution leverages Snowflake Document AI to extract structured data from unstructured PDF statements using a small labeled corpus (approximately 20 documents). Extracted data are reconciled against authoritative source-of-truth datasets to identify discrepancies at scale. Results are surfaced through interactive dashboards and automated reports. The framework enables population-level testing rather than sampling-based approaches, improving audit coverage and supporting continuous assurance objectives. Recent advances in document intelligence and analytics-driven audit frameworks enable scalable, near real-time risk identification and continuous assurance.

### [156] [Bridging Generation and Training: A Systematic Review of Quality Issues in LLMs for Code](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05267)
*Kaifeng He,Xiaojun Zhang,Peiliang Cai,Mingwei Liu,Yanlin Wang,Chong Wang,Kaifeng Huang,Bihuan Chen,Xin Peng,Zibin Zheng*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该论文通过114篇研究的系统文献综述，建立了训练数据质量问题与代码生成缺陷之间的因果映射框架，提出了一套统一分类法，并揭示了质量保证从被动修复向主动数据治理转变的趋势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在代码生成中频繁产生缺陷（从逻辑错误到安全漏洞），而这些缺陷的根源常被归因于模型层面，但实证证据表明其根本原因在于训练语料库的质量问题。然而，训练数据质量问题如何具体传导至生成代码质量缺陷的机制尚未被系统映射。

Method: 对114篇主要研究进行系统文献综述，建立统一的分类法（将生成代码质量问题分为9个维度，训练数据质量问题分为代码属性和非代码属性），形式化定义了18种典型的传播映射机制，并综合了数据、模型和生成生命周期各阶段的检测与缓解技术。

Result: 揭示了质量保证方法论的明确转变：从反应式、基于启发式的生成后过滤，转向主动式、以数据为中心的治理和闭环修复。建立了训练数据质量与生成代码质量之间的因果映射框架。

Conclusion: 识别了当前开放挑战，并提出了通过集成数据整理和持续评估来开发可靠LLM代码生成的研究方向。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) frequently generate defective outputs in code generation tasks, ranging from logical bugs to security vulnerabilities. While these generation failures are often treated as model-level limitations, empirical evidence increasingly traces their root causes to imperfections within the training corpora. Yet, the specific mechanisms linking training data quality issues to generated code quality issues remain largely unmapped. This paper presents a systematic literature review of 114 primary studies to investigate how training data quality issues propagate into code generation. We establish a unified taxonomy that categorizes generated code quality issues across nine dimensions and training data quality issues into code and non-code attributes. Based on this taxonomy, we formalize a causal framework detailing 18 typical propagation mapping mechanisms. Furthermore, we synthesize state-of-the-art detection and mitigation techniques across the data, model, and generation lifecycles. The reviewed literature reveals a clear methodological shift: quality assurance is transitioning from reactive, heuristic-based post-generation filtering toward proactive, data-centric governance and closed-loop repair. Finally, we identify open challenges and outline research directions for developing reliable LLMs for code through integrated data curation and continuous evaluation. Our repository is available at https://github.com/SYSUSELab/From-Data-to-Code.

</details>


### [157] [Is this Build Failure Related to my Patch? An Empirical Study of Unrelated Build Failures in Continuous Integration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05564)
*Andie Huang,Daniel Alencar da Costa,Grant Dick,Mariam El Mezouar*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文研究了77,354次CI构建失败，发现开发者平均花费4小时判断失败是否与自己的代码推送相关。通过提取33个特征并构建半监督PU学习模型，成功预测不相关的构建失败，F1分数达0.44-0.91，AUC达0.63-0.97。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CI系统中并发构建常导致构建失败与触发推送无关，开发者需花费大量时间判断失败是否可操作，浪费开发效率。

Method: 分析了7个Apache开源项目的77,354次构建失败，对371个确认不相关的失败进行文档分析；提取33个特征（包括CI延迟、重复错误信息、评论数量等），构建半监督正例-无标签（PU）学习模型进行预测。

Result: 模型在7个Apache项目上达到精确率0.70-0.88，召回率0.30-1.00，F1分数0.44-0.91，AUC 0.63-0.97。CI延迟、重复错误信息和前置评论数量是重要预测特征。

Conclusion: PU学习模型能够有效帮助开发者识别与当前代码推送无关的构建失败，减少不必要的问题排查时间。

Abstract: Continuous Integration (CI) systems often run many builds concurrently. In this setting, a legitimate build failure may not be caused by the code push that triggered it. Such unrelated build failures can waste developer effort because developers must determine whether the failure is actionable for their current change. We study 77,354 CI build failures from seven open source Apache projects to understand and predict unrelated build failures. We find that developers spend a median of 4 hours identifying whether a failure is related or unrelated to their push. We also perform a document analysis of 371 confirmed unrelated build failures sampled from 10,316 potentially unrelated failures. The analysis shows that unrelated test failures account for 20% of the cases in which developers classify build failures as unrelated. To predict unrelated build failures, we extract 33 features from issue reports, issue comments, and commits associated with the triggering push. We build semi-supervised Positive and Unlabeled (PU) learning models for seven Apache projects. The models achieve precision from 0.70 to 0.88, recall from 0.30 to 1.00, F1-score from 0.44 to 0.91, and AUC from 0.63 to 0.97. Feature importance analysis shows that CI latency, repeated error messages, and the number of preceding comments are useful indicators of unrelated build failures. These results show that PU learning can help developers identify build failures that are unlikely to be caused by their current push.

</details>


### [158] [An Empirical Study of Proactive Coding Assistants in Real-World Software Development](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05700)
*Lehui Li,Ruixuan Jia,Guo-Ye Yang,Jia Li*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文通过收集1,246名专业开发者的真实IDE交互数据，发现LLM模拟的编码行为与真实行为在多样性、时间结构和探索模式上存在显著差距，并构建了ProCodeBench基准，证明基于模拟数据的评估会高估模型在真实场景中的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM编码助手多为被动响应式，缺乏主动推断开发者意图的能力；而该方向研究受限于缺乏大规模真实开发者行为数据，现有研究普遍使用LLM模拟IDE轨迹，但其真实保真度未知。

Method: 通过自定义VS Code扩展收集1,246名资深开发者连续三天的真实IDE交互轨迹，并构建对应的LLM模拟轨迹进行比较分析；基于收集的真实数据构建ProCodeBench基准，评估多种模型在该基准上的主动意图预测能力。

Result: 模拟轨迹与真实轨迹在行为多样性、时间结构和探索模式上存在显著差异；当前主流模型在真实IDE轨迹上的主动意图预测性能远不理想，模拟数据会高估真实表现；模拟数据不能替代真实数据，但可在微调前作为补充。

Conclusion: 真实开发者行为数据对评估和训练主动编码助手至关重要，基于模拟数据的评估可能产生误导性结论。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM)-based coding assistants have made substantial progress, yet most systems remain reactive, requiring developers to explicitly formulate their needs. Proactive coding assistants aim to infer latent developer intent from integrated development environment (IDE) interactions and repository context, thereby reducing interaction overhead and supporting more seamless assistance. However, research in this direction is limited by the scarcity of large-scale real-world developer behavior data. Existing studies therefore often rely on LLM-simulated IDE traces, whose fidelity to real development behavior remains unclear. In this paper, we investigate this simulation-to-reality gap through a large-scale empirical study. We collect real IDE interaction traces from 1{,}246 experienced industry developers over three consecutive days using a custom Visual Studio Code extension, and construct paired LLM-simulated traces for controlled comparison. Our analysis shows that simulated traces differ substantially from real traces in behavioral diversity, temporal structure, and exploratory patterns. Based on the collected data, we introduce \textbf{ProCodeBench}, a real-world benchmark for proactive intent prediction. Experiments with representative LLMs, retrieval-augmented methods, and agentic baselines show that current approaches remain far from reliable under real IDE traces, suggesting that simulation-based evaluation can overestimate real-world performance. Finally, our training study shows that simulated data cannot replace real data, but can complement it when used before real-world fine-tuning. These findings highlight the importance of real developer behavior data for evaluating and training proactive coding assistants.

</details>


### [159] [On Fixing Insecure AI-Generated Code through Model Fine-Tuning and Prompting Strategies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05867)
*Ali Soltanian Fard Jahromi,Amjed Tahir,Peng Liang,Foutse Khomh*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了提升AI生成代码安全性的多种策略（微调与提示工程），发现安全改进高度依赖策略和模型，且修复漏洞时常引入新问题，不存在通用解决方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI生成代码虽性能优异但存在大量安全漏洞，现有缓解方法效果不稳定，亟需系统性评估不同策略的实际效果及其副作用。

Method: 针对CWE列表，采用微调和提示工程两种方法对模型输出进行精炼，在多模型、多编程语言上评估安全改进效果，并分析漏洞严重性、共现关系及修复副作用。

Result: 安全改进高度依赖具体策略和模型；修复特定漏洞时常引入新的弱点；没有任何策略能在所有模型和场景下一致消除漏洞。

Conclusion: 目前不存在"防弹"的通用安全解决方案，未来需要更精细、更自适应的安全加固方法。

Abstract: The security of AI-generated code remains a major obstacle to its widespread adoption. Although code generation models achieve strong performance on functional benchmarks, their outputs frequently contain bugs and security weaknesses that undermine their trustworthiness. Prior work has explored a range of approaches to mitigate security issues in AI-generated code, e.g., using static analysis-guided generation and prompt engineering. However, their effectiveness varies widely across models and settings. This paper presents a systematic investigation of strategies for hardening model-generated code against a list of Common Weakness Enumeration (CWE). We assess the extent to which these strategies improve security across models and programming languages, using fine-tuning and prompting approaches for model output refinement. Beyond the prevalence of security weaknesses, we analyse the severity of identified CWEs, their co-occurrence, and the unintended consequences of remediation (i.e., whether fixing certain weaknesses introduces new weaknesses elsewhere in the same code). Our results show that security improvements are highly strategy- and model-dependent. Although some approaches reduce specific classes of weaknesses, they often introduce new weaknesses as side effects of the fixes. Moreover, no strategy consistently eliminates weaknesses across all models and scenarios, highlighting the absence of a universally effective "bulletproof" solution for secure AI-generated code.

</details>


### [160] [Evaluating Non-English Developer Support in Machine Learning for Software Engineering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05902)
*Jonathan Katzy,Yongcheng Huang,Gopal-Raj Panchu,Maksym Ziemlewski,Paris Loizides,Sander Vermeulen,Arie van Deursen,Maliheh Izadi*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文研究了非英语代码注释生成及其评估问题，发现模型在多语言场景下性能显著下降，且现有自动评估方法（包括神经指标和LLM评判）均无法可靠检测错误，人类判断仍然不可或缺。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前代码生成与评估主要基于英语，缺乏对多语言开发场景（代码包含非英语自然语言）的理解，存在研究空白。

Method: 评估5个代码LLM在5种自然语言上的注释生成能力；对12,500条生成注释进行开放编码研究，构建人工标注数据集和26类错误分类体系；评估神经指标和LLM评判管线的性能。

Result: 非英语场景下生成性能严重下降，语言错误增加最多15.1倍；所有自动评估方法均无法可靠检测非英语注释中的错误，神经指标甚至无法区分正确注释、错误输出或随机噪声。

Conclusion: 多语言工具的关键障碍在于评估和生成两个方面，人类判断在当前阶段仍不可或缺。

Abstract: Large Language Models are increasingly used in software engineering, but both code generation and its evaluation remain predominantly English-centric. This leaves a major gap in our understanding of how well current tools support multilingual development, where code contains non-English natural language. In this paper, we investigate non-English code comment generation and the reliability of current methods for evaluating such outputs. We evaluate five code LLMs (CodeGemma, CodeLlama, CodeQwen1.5, GraniteCode, and StarCoder2) across five natural languages: Dutch, English, Greek, Polish and Chinese. We further conduct an open-coding study of 12,500 generated comments, from which we derive a publicly released human-annotated dataset and a taxonomy of 26 error types. We use these human annotations, to evaluate the performance of neural metrics, and LLM-as-a-judge pipelines.
  Our findings show that generative performance deteriorates substantially outside English, with linguistic errors increasing by up to 15.1$\times$, alongside frequent incoherent generations and a rise in semantic errors. More critically, we show that detecting errors in non-English comments underperforms. Across classical overlap-based metrics, off-the-shelf neural metrics, extended neural metrics using newer multilingual, language-specific, and code-specific models, and LLM-as-a-judge pipelines, no automatic approach provides reliable and consistent assessment. Neural metrics fail to distinguish correct comments from incorrect outputs or even random noise, and tend to overestimate quality in non-English settings. LLM-as-a-judge methods achieve the highest agreement with human annotations but fail to reliably capture important language-related and semantic errors. Overall, our results show that evaluation and generation are key barriers for multilingual tooling, and that human judgment remains indispensable.

</details>


### [161] [Schedule-and-Calibrate: Utility-Guided Multi-Task Reinforcement Learning for Code LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06111)
*Yujia Chen,Yang Ye,Xiao Chu,Yuchi Ma,Cuiyun Gao*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 提出ASTOR框架，通过效用驱动的分层数据调度和自适应策略优化，实现多任务代码强化学习训练，在单个模型上超越任务专属专家9.0%-9.5%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MTRL方法将所有编码任务统一处理，依赖固定数据课程和共享优化策略，限制了多任务训练的有效性；且部署多个任务专属专家成本高昂。

Method: 提出ASTOR框架，包含两个耦合模块：1) 分层效用路由数据调度模块，分层分配训练预算并优先选择有信息量的提示；2) 自适应效用校准策略优化模块，动态缩放每个任务的KL正则化，匹配当前训练状态。

Result: 在两个LLM上，ASTOR在四个编码任务中一致提升单一模型性能，超越最佳任务专属专家9.0%-9.5%，超越最强MTRL基线7.5%-12.8%。

Conclusion: 基于任务效用的多任务协调框架能有效提升统一模型在多编码任务上的表现，降低部署成本的同时取得更优性能。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) with verifiable rewards has proven effective at post-training LLMs for coding, yet deploying separate task-specific specialists incurs costs that scale with the number of tasks, motivating a unified multi-task RL (MTRL) approach. However, existing MTRL methods treat all coding tasks uniformly, relying on fixed data curricula under a shared optimization strategy, ultimately limiting the effectiveness of multi-task training. To address these limitations, we propose ASTOR, a multi-tASk code reinforcement learning framework via uTility-driven coORdination. Centered on task utility, a signal capturing each task learning potential and cross-task synergy, ASTOR comprises two coupled modules: 1) Hierarchical Utility-Routed Data Scheduling module hierarchically allocates training budget and prioritizes informative prompts, steering training toward the most valuable data and 2) Adaptive Utility-Calibrated Policy Optimization module dynamically scales per-task KL regularization, matching update constraints to each tasks current training state. Experiments on two widely-used LLMs across four representative coding tasks demonstrate that ASTOR consistently improves a single model across all tasks, outperforming the best task-specific specialist by 9.0%-9.5% and surpassing the strongest MTRL baseline by 7.5%-12.8%.

</details>


### [162] [Breaking, Stale, or Missing? Benchmarking Coding Agents on Project-Level Test Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06125)
*Ye Shang,Quanjun Zhang,Haichuan Hu,Chunrong Fang,Liang Xiao,Zhenyu Chen*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: TEBench 是首个项目级别的测试演化基准测试，包含314个来自10个项目的任务实例，覆盖三种演化类型（测试失效、测试过时、测试缺失）。评估表明，现有框架（Claude Code、Codex CLI、OpenCode）在识别F1上均收敛于45.7%-49.4%，其中测试过时最困难（F1约36%），且存在反应式"执行-失败-修复"循环的固有局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有测试演化基准测试仅在方法级别操作且提供预配对输入，绕过了从完整项目中定位受影响测试的任务，且完全排除了新增测试的需求。因此需要一个真实项目级别的基准测试来推动测试演化研究。

Method: 通过四阶段流水线基于Defects4J项目构建TEBench，包含314个任务实例，每个实例标注三种演化类型（Test-Breaking、Test-Stale、Test-Missing）。评估了覆盖三个工业智能体框架（Claude Code、Codex CLI、OpenCode）和六个基础模型的七个配置，以及一个启发式基线。

Result: 所有七个配置在识别F1上收敛于45.7%-49.4%；Test-Stale最困难（F1约36%）；生成的测试修改可执行但与真实方案差异较大；存在反应式"执行-失败-修复"循环的固有局限。

Conclusion: 现有框架在测试演化任务上存在性能天花板，尤其是无法处理测试过时和测试缺失类型，需要新的方法突破反应式循环的局限。

Abstract: As production code evolves, the test suite must co-evolve to remain effective. Existing benchmarks for test evolution operate at method-level granularity with pre-paired inputs, bypassing the task of locating affected tests from the full project and excluding the need for new tests entirely. We present TEBench, the first project-level benchmark for test evolution. Given a project repository and a code-changing commit, TEBench requires systems to autonomously identify tests requiring modification, determine where new tests are needed, and produce the corresponding test patch. We construct TEBench through a four-stage pipeline over Defects4J projects, curating 314 task instances from 10 projects with developer-written ground truth. Each instance is annotated with one or more of three evolution types: Test-Breaking (tests that fail), Test-Stale (tests that pass but no longer meaningfully validate updated behavior), and Test-Missing (new tests needed for introduced behavior). We evaluate seven configurations spanning three industrial agent frameworks (Claude Code, Codex CLI, OpenCode) and six base models, alongside a heuristic baseline. All seven configurations converge on an identification F1 of 45.7% to 49.4%, revealing a shared performance ceiling across both frameworks and base models. Test-Stale is the most challenging type, averaging F1 around 36%, since configurations rely on execution failure signals and lack proactive semantic reasoning. On the update task, configurations produce highly executable test modifications whose surface form diverges substantially from ground truth. Trajectory analysis reveals a reactive "execute-fail-fix" loop that succeeds for breaking tests but structurally cannot address stale or missing tests. TEBench is available at https://github.com/iSEngLab/TEBench with a leaderboard at https://tebench-leadership.vercel.app.

</details>


### [163] [BUILD-AND-FIND: An Effort-Aware Protocol for Evaluating Agent-Managed Codebases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06136)
*Jhen-Ke Lin*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 提出BUILD-AND-FIND协议，用于评估代码生成仓库的下游可恢复性（即后续智能体能否从生成的代码仓库中找回原始设计意图），并分离行为正确性与工件侧意图恢复能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码智能体评测主要关注生成代码的行为正确性，但仓库级工程中，生成的仓库不仅是任务答案，更是未来工作的沟通工件。即使行为正确，不同仓库在暴露设计意图方面存在差异，缺乏评估这种差异的标准化方法。

Method: BUILD-AND-FIND协议：构建者根据隐藏规范创建代码库；查找者仅凭代码库+规范追溯的多选题作答。报告恢复准确率、可重复性、实现覆盖率和检查工作量。通过问题-only和规范-only对照控制先验，审计区分遗漏声明与查找者失败。

Result: 在发布的高先验任务包中，恢复准确率接近饱和，因此检查工作量和查找者特定效应成为主要区分指标。

Conclusion: 该协议有效分离了行为正确性与工件侧意图恢复能力，提供了评估代码仓库作为沟通工件的标准化方法，即使行为正确性已很高的场景下，仍可通过检查工作量等指标区分不同仓库的沟通质量。

Abstract: Most coding-agent benchmarks ask whether generated code behaves correctly. That remains essential, but repository-level engineering is increasingly agent-managed: one agent writes a repository, and later agents inspect, audit, or extend it as working context. In that setting, a generated repository is not only an answer to a task but also a communication artifact for future work. Even when strong agents nearly satisfy the visible behavioral objective, repositories can differ in how clearly they expose the intended behavior and design choices behind that behavior. We introduce BUILD-AND-FIND, a protocol for evaluating whether downstream agents can recover those intended choices from generated repositories, and how much inspection that recovery requires. For each task, a builder sees a hidden repository specification and creates a codebase; a finder sees only the codebase and a specification-traced multiple-choice question bank. The protocol separates behavioral correctness from artifact-side recovery and reports recovery accuracy, repeatability, implementation coverage, and inspection effort. Accuracy and stability act as gates: effort is interpreted only when recovery succeeds reliably. Among artifacts from which the same intent can be recovered, lower effort by the same finder suggests that the artifact makes that intent easier to locate. Question-only and spec-only controls quantify generic priors and specification access, while audits separate omitted claims from finder failures and check whether correct answers cite artifact evidence. In the released high-prior task pack, recovery accuracy is near saturation, so inspection effort and finder-specific effects provide the main panel-local comparison.

</details>


### [164] [Teaching LLMs Program Semantics via Symbolic Execution Traces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06184)
*Jonas Bayer,Stefan Zetzsche,Olivier Bouissou,Remi Delmas,Michael Tautschnig,Soonho Kong*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出基于SV-COMP 2025的500个C验证任务评估框架，发现模型在违规检测上存在严重短板。通过用符号执行引擎Soteria生成的约3000个bug traces对Qwen3-8B进行持续预训练，结合思维链推理，将违规检测准确率提升17个百分点，效果优于4倍大的Qwen3-32B模型，且trace训练与思维链具有超加性协同效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有模型在C程序验证任务中整体准确率高，但违规检测能力薄弱且随程序长度急剧下降，存在严重不平衡性。为弥补这一缺陷，探索利用形式化验证trace数据训练模型。

Method: 构建基于SV-COMP 2025的500个C验证任务评估框架，包含五种属性类型。使用Soteria符号执行引擎在通用开源C代码上生成验证trace，对Qwen3-8B进行持续预训练，并结合思维链推理提升违规检测能力。

Result: 仅约3000个bug traces结合思维链推理，使违规检测提升17+百分点；训练的8B模型在违规检测上超越4倍大的Qwen3-32B（无思维链）；trace训练与思维链具有超加性协同效应；改进泛化到所有五种属性类型。

Conclusion: 形式化验证trace训练能显著提升模型在程序验证中违规检测的平衡性，且trace语义（而非代码量）是提升关键，trace的 curation 和格式也很重要。

Abstract: We introduce an evaluation framework of 500 C verification tasks across five property types (memory safety, overflow, termination, reachability, data races) built on SV-COMP 2025, and evaluate 14 models across six families. We find that high overall accuracy masks a critical weakness: while most models reliably confirm properties hold, violation detection varies widely and degrades sharply with program length. To close this gap, we train on formal verification artifacts: running the Soteria symbolic execution engine on generic open-source C code and using the resulting traces for continued pretraining of Qwen3-8B. Just ${\sim}$3,000 bug traces combined with chain-of-thought reasoning at inference time improve violation detection by over 17 percentage points, producing one of the most balanced accuracy profiles among evaluated models. On violation detection, the trained 8B model outperforms the 4$\times$ larger Qwen3-32B without thinking and approaches it in overall accuracy. The interaction between trace training and chain-of-thought is superadditive: neither alone provides meaningful gains, but their combination does. Improvements transfer across all five property types, including ones the training traces do not target. Our 28 configurations confirm the gains stem from trace semantics, not code volume, and that trace curation and format matter.

### [165] [SiblingRepair: Sibling-Based Multi-Hunk Repair with Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06209)
*Xinyu Liu,Jiayu Ren,Yusen Wang,Qi Xin,Xiaoyuan Xie,Jifeng Xuan*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: SiblingRepair是一种基于LLM的多hunk自动程序修复技术，专门用于修复代码中相似位置（siblings）的同类错误，显著优于现有方法Hercules。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开发者在实现相关功能时经常在多个代码位置（siblings）犯相似错误，需要一致的修复。现有SOTA方法Hercules存在强假设（如兄弟位置和提交历史可用性）、僵化的AST匹配和模板化补丁生成等局限。

Method: 从频谱定位的疑似位置出发，使用token和嵌入匹配搜索语义相似的兄弟候选；利用LLM识别失败相关的兄弟，通过两种策略生成一致补丁：联合修复（同时修复多个兄弟）和迭代修复（渐进分析候选）；保留早期位置的候选补丁并组合成多hunk补丁。

Result: 在Defects4J和GHRB基准测试上，SiblingRepair显著优于包括Hercules在内的SOTA多hunk修复技术。消融实验验证了其兄弟检测和修复组件的有效性，并排除了LLM数据泄漏的显著影响。

Conclusion: SiblingRepair通过结合语义匹配与LLM，有效克服了现有方法的局限，推动了兄弟位置修复和通用多hunk修复技术的发展。

Abstract: Developers often make similar mistakes across code locations implementing related functionalities. These locations, called siblings, share similar issues and require similar fixes. Accurately identifying siblings and consistently repairing them are crucial for automated program repair. Hercules is a SOTA technique designed for sibling repair. However, it is limited by strong assumptions about sibling locations and commit-history availability, rigid AST-based sibling matching, and inflexible template-based patch generation. To address these limitations, we present SiblingRepair, a new LLM-based multi-hunk APR technique specialized for sibling repair. Starting from a suspicious location identified by spectrum-based fault localization, SiblingRepair searches for semantically related sibling candidates using token- and embedding-based code matching, without restricting discovery to failing-test coverage or commit history. It then uses an LLM to identify failure-relevant siblings and generate consistent patches through two complementary strategies: simultaneous repair, which jointly repairs siblings, and iterative repair, which progressively analyzes candidates for patch construction. SiblingRepair further preserves promising patches generated from earlier suspicious locations and combines them into generalized multi-hunk patches. We evaluate SiblingRepair on the Defects4J and GHRB benchmarks. The results show that SiblingRepair substantially outperforms SOTA multi-hunk repair techniques including Hercules. Our evaluation further demonstrates its repair efficiency, the effectiveness of its sibling detection and repair components, and limited impact of the LLM data leakage on the results. Overall, SiblingRepair advances automated sibling and general multi-hunk repair.

</details>


### [166] [Correct Code, Vulnerable Dependencies: A Large Scale Measurement Study of LLM-Specified Library Versions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06279)
*Chengjie Wang,Jingzheng Wu,Xiang Ling,Tianyue Luo,Chen Zhao*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文首次大规模测量了LLM生成的Python代码中第三方库版本选择的安全与兼容性风险。研究发现LLM倾向于指定版本标识符，但其中大量版本存在已知CVE漏洞（36.70%-55.70%），且多数漏洞在模型知识截止前已公开。静态兼容率低至19.70%-63.20%，动态测试通过率仅6.49%-48.62%。研究表明版本选择存在系统性偏差，是一个被忽视的风险面。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM生成的代码中常用第三方库版本信息，但这些版本选择可能引入安全漏洞和兼容性问题，此前缺乏系统性研究。

Method: 评估10个LLM在PinTrace基准（1000个Stack Overflow编程任务）上的表现，测量版本指定率、CVE暴露率、兼容性（静态和动态）等指标，并进行归因实验。

Result: LLM版本指定率26.83%-95.18%（直接提示），降至6.45%-59.19%（创建清单文件）。36.70%-55.70%的任务包含已知CVE，其中62.75%-74.51%为严重或高危。72.27%-91.37%的CVE在模型知识截止前已公开。静态兼容率19.70%-63.20%，动态通过率6.49%-48.62%。外部锚定的版本约束可显著降低风险。

Conclusion: LLM版本选择是一个被忽视的一级风险面，存在系统性偏差，外部约束可缓解问题。研究已公开并与模型社区共享发现。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are now largely involved in software development workflows, and the code they generate routinely includes third-party library (TPL) imports annotated with specific version identifiers. These version choices can carry security and compatibility risks, yet they have not been systematically studied.
  We present the first large-scale measurement study of version-level risk in LLM-generated Python code, evaluating 10 LLMs on PinTrace, a curated benchmark of 1,000 Stack Overflow programming tasks. LLMs tend to specify version identifiers when directly prompted at 26.83%-95.18%, while down to 6.45%-59.19% in creating a manifest file directly. Among the specified versions, 36.70%-55.70% of tasks contain at least one known CVE, and 62.75%-74.51% of them carry Critical or High severity ratings. In 72.27%-91.37% of cases, the associated CVEs were publicly disclosed before the model's knowledge cutoff. The statistics show all models converge on the same small set of risky release versions, indicating a systemic bias rather than isolated model error. Static compatibility rates range from 19.70% to 63.20%, with installation failure as the dominant cause. The dynamic test cases confirm the pattern by 6.49%-48.62% pass rates. Further experiments confirm that these failures are attributable to version selection rather than code quality, and that externally anchored version constraints substantially reduce both vulnerability exposure and compatibility failures. Our findings reveal LLM version selection as a first-class, previously overlooked risk surface in LLM-based development. We disclosed these findings to the community of the evaluated models, and several confirmed the issue. All the code and dataset have been released for open science at https://github.com/dw763j/PinTrace.

</details>

### [167] [Auto Research with Specialist Agents Develops Effective and Non-Trivial Training Recipes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05724)
*Jingjie Ning,Xiaochuan Li,Ji Zeng,Hao Kang,Chenyan Xiong*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种自动化科研闭环系统，通过外部测量驱动假设、代码编辑、实验和反馈的迭代循环，实现了无需人工干预的自主科研探索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动科研方法多关注生成论文或单一模型检查点，缺乏可审计的完整实验轨迹和闭环反馈机制。本文旨在构建一个由外部评估驱动的闭环实证循环，使智能体能够利用实验反馈（包括失败信息）进行程序级改进。

Method: 构建一个封闭的实证循环：每个试验包含假设、可执行代码编辑、评估者拥有的结果以及塑造下一次提案的反馈。使用专业智能体划分配方空间并共享实验谱系。通过1,197次主试验和600次对照试验，完全由系统自主运行，无人工干预。

Result: 在三个主要任务上取得显著改进：Parameter Golf验证bpb降低0.81%，NanoChat-D12 CORE提升38.7%，CIFAR-10 Airbench96墙钟时间减少4.59%。系统自主生成了157次架构域审计和程序重写（如注意力核路径更改）。

Conclusion: 该闭环系统能够自主编写代码、提交实验、吸收反馈、应用和组合已知技术，并在无需人工选择提案、编辑配方或修复失败试验的情况下改进公共起始配方，展示了自动化科研的可行性。

Abstract: We study auto research as a closed empirical loop driven by external measurement. Each submitted trial carries a hypothesis, an executable code edit, an evaluator-owned outcome, and feedback that shapes the next proposal. The output is not a generated paper or a single model checkpoint, but an auditable trajectory of proposals, code diffs, experiments, scores, and failure labels. We instantiate this loop with specialist agents that partition recipe surfaces and share measured lineage across trials. The central empirical finding is that lineage feedback lets agents turn evaluator outcomes, including crashes, budget overruns, size failures, and accuracy-gate misses, into later program-level recipe edits rather than one-shot suggestions. Across 1,197 headline-run trials plus 600 Parameter Golf control trials after one-time setup and launch, humans did not choose proposals, edit recipes, override scores, or repair failed trials during the search. In the three headline runs, the same submitted-trial loop reduces Parameter Golf validation bpb by $0.81\%$, raises NanoChat-D12 CORE by $38.7\%$, and reduces CIFAR-10 Airbench96 wallclock by $4.59\%$, with each task measured by its own external evaluator and legality checks. The trace includes a strict architecture-domain audit of 157 headline-run submissions and program rewrites such as a NanoChat attention-kernel path change. Within this scope the loop autonomously writes code, submits experiments, absorbs feedback, applies and combines known techniques inside each environment, and improves public starting recipes.

</details>


### [168] [Multiagent Stochastic Shortest Path Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06056)
*Martin Jonáš,Antonín Kučera,Vojtěch Kůr,Jan Mačák,Vojtěch Řehák*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有单智能体随机最短路径问题已有较多研究，但多智能体协作场景下的最优策略问题尚缺乏系统分析，特别是在自主和协调两种不同设置下的计算与策略复杂性对比。

Method: 对MSSP问题进行形式化建模，分别分析自主（无通信）和协调（可通信协作）两种设置下的计算复杂性和策略复杂性，并设计相应的高效策略合成算法，最后通过实验与自然基线方法进行比较。

We analyze the computational and strategy-complexity of the problem in both autonomous and coordinated settings, and we design efficient strategy-synthesis algorithms. The algorithms are experimentally evaluated on instances of increasing size against natural baselines.

### [169] [Power-Efficiency and Scalability Analysis of Magnetically-Actuated Satellite Swarms via Convex Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06286)
*Yuta Takahashi,Seang Shim,Hiraku Sakamoto,Shin-ichiro Sakai*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于凸优化的评估框架，用于分析由磁场相互作用维持的卫星集群孔径的功耗问题。研究发现，增加卫星数量可以提高编队保持的功率效率，表明磁驱动集群架构是构建大型空间系统的节能替代方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 卫星集群构成的分布式孔径具有高增益、窄波束和大孔径等优势，但长期维持编队面临轨道动力学不稳定和电磁力非线性带来的功耗约束非凸问题，使得系统级配置分析困难。

Method: 开发了一个基于凸优化的框架，用于分析大型磁驱动卫星集群的功耗，将非凸的电磁力/力矩非线性约束转化为可处理的问题。

Result: 分析表明，增加卫星数量可以提高编队保持的功率效率。

Conclusion: 磁驱动集群架构为构建大型空间系统提供了一种比传统少卫星电磁编队飞行方案更节能的选择。

Abstract: This correspondence presents a convex-optimization-based evaluation framework of satellite-swarm-based apertures maintained by magnetic-field interactions. Spaceborne distributed apertures are composed of multiple satellites and are attractive for scientific and commercial missions because their scalability enables high-gain, narrow-beam, and large-aperture capabilities beyond the launch-size limitations. A key challenge is that the long-term maintenance of such virtual structures requires consistent formation control amid unstable orbital dynamics, and magnetic interactions generated by satellite-mounted magnetorquers offer a desirable propellant-free position-control strategy. However, the nonlinearities of the electromagnetic force and torque model lead to a nonconvex power-consumption constraint, making system-level configuration analysis difficult. To address this issue, we develop a convex optimization-based framework to analyze the power consumption of large magnetically actuated satellite swarms. The resulting analysis shows that increasing the number of satellites can improve formation-keeping power efficiency. This indicates that magnetically actuated swarm architectures provide a power-efficient alternative to the conventional few-satellite electromagnetic formation-flight concept for constructing large-scale space systems.

### [170] [Improving the Efficiency of Language Agent Teams with Adaptive Task Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06320)
*Elizabeth Mieczkowski,Alexander Ku,Tiwalayo Eisape,Dilip Arumugam,John Matters,Katherine M. Collins,Ilia Sucholutsky,Thomas L. Griffiths*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM团队协调方法要么过于僵化（预定义角色/流水线），要么过于松散（无结构团队导致冲突和资源浪费），缺乏平衡适应性与效率的方案。

Method: LATTE让智能体团队共同维护一个共享的动态协调图，编码子任务依赖、智能体分配和进度状态，在部分可观测和通信约束下实现动态工作分配与任务发现。

Result: 在多项协作任务和多种基座模型上，LATTE减少了token消耗、墙钟时间、通信量和协调失败（如文件冲突、冗余输出），同时匹配或超越MetaGPT、去中心化团队、Leader-Worker层级和静态分解等方法的准确率。

Conclusion: 基于分布式系统启发的动态协调图方法能有效平衡LLM团队的适应性与效率，为多智能体协作提供了新的设计范式。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed in teams, yet existing coordination approaches often occupy two extremes. Highly structured methods rely on fixed roles, pipelines, or task decompositions assigned a priori. In contrast, fully unstructured teams enable adaptability and exploration but suffer from inefficiencies such as error propagation, inter-agent conflicts, and wasted resources (measured in time, tokens, or file operations). We introduce Language Agent Teams for Task Evolution (LATTE), a framework for coordinating LLM teams inspired by distributed systems, where processors must operate under partial observability and communication constraints. In LATTE, a team of agents collaboratively construct and maintain a shared, evolving coordination graph which encodes sub-task dependencies, individual agent assignment, and the current state of sub-task progress. This protocol maintains consistency while empowering agents to dynamically allocate work, adapt coordination, and discover new tasks. Across multiple collaborative tasks and a variety of base models, we demonstrate how LATTE reduces token usage, wall-clock time, communication, and coordination failures (e.g. file conflicts and redundant outputs) while matching or exceeding the accuracy of standard designs including MetaGPT, decentralized teams, top-down Leader-Worker hierarchies, and static decompositions.

### [171] [Coordination Matters: Evaluation of Cooperative Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06557)
*Maria Ana Cardei,Matthew Landers,Afsaneh Doryab*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出协调感知评估视角，通过STAT测试平台分析多智能体强化学习中返回值相同但协调机制不同的情况，强调过程级诊断指标（如冗余分配、任务效率）对评估协作质量的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MARL基准过度依赖返回值、成功率等聚合指标，无法揭示智能体间的实际协调机制，尤其在任务规模组合爆炸时。

Method: 提出STAT测试平台（受约束承诺的空间任务分配），固定观测与任务规则，系统变化智能体数、任务数和环境规模，评估六种代表性基于价值的MARL方法。

Result: 相似返回值下存在不同的协调机制（冗余分配差异、分配多样性、任务完成效率）；规模扩展受限于动作空间大小、分配压力、稀疏决策机会及相互依赖智能体间的冗余选择。

Conclusion: 协调感知评估应作为返回值基准的必要补充，以更全面评估合作MARL方法。

Abstract: Cooperative multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) benchmarks commonly emphasize aggregate outcomes such as return, success rate, or completion time. While essential, these metrics often fail to reveal how agents coordinate, particularly in settings where agents, tasks, and joint assignment choices scale combinatorially. We propose a coordination-aware evaluation perspective that supplements return with process-level diagnostics. We instantiate this perspective using STAT, a controlled commitment-constrained spatial task-allocation testbed that systematically varies agents, tasks, and environment size while holding observation access and task rules fixed. We evaluate six representative value-based MARL methods across varying levels of centralization. Our results show that similar return trends can reflect distinct coordination mechanisms, including differences in redundant assignment, assignment diversity, and task-completion efficiency. We find that in commitment-constrained task allocation, performance under scale is shaped not only by nominal action-space size, but also by assignment pressure, sparse decision opportunities, and redundant choices among interdependent agents. Our findings motivate coordination-aware evaluation as a necessary complement to return-based benchmarking for cooperative MARL.
